  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_afdd7f58-eae9-4cc0-8775-5b8fff72638c'
      });

  <span id="freeText7468470347779397534" style="display:none"><i>“Walaupun tidak ada hal lain di dunia ini yang bisa kaupercayai, percayalah bahwa aku mencintaimu. Sepenuh hatiku.”</i><br /><br />Ini adalah salah satu kisah yang terjadi di bawah langit kota New York…<br />Ini kisah tentang harapan yang muncul di tengah keputusasaan…<br />Tentang impian yang bertahan di antara keraguan…<br />Dan tentang cinta yang memberikan alasan untuk bertahan hidup.<br /><br />Awalnya Alex Hirano lebih memilih jauh-jauh dari gadis itu—malaikat kegelapannya yang sudah membuatnya cacat.<br />Kemudian Mia Clark tertawa dan Alex bertanya-tanya bagaimana ia dulu bisa berpikir gadis yang memiliki tawa secerah matahari itu adalah malaikat kegelapannya.<br /><br />Awalnya mata hitam yang menatapnya dengan tajam dan dingin itu membuat Mia gemetar ketakutan dan berharap bumi menelannya detik itu juga.<br />Kemudian Alex Hirano tersenyum dan jantung Mia yang malang melonjak dan berdebar begitu keras sampai Mia takut Alex bisa mendengarnya.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16710273669648898181">I CRIED. well i guess it's not a surprise, because i've known Ilana Tan as someone who can write a story that plays well with the reader's heart. and i think this book is BETTER than - if not as good as - the 4 Seasons series. the story is not that complicated actually, but the emotions are just unbelievable! i still can't believe how much i cried while finishing the book... i've been reading a lot of emotional books lately, but this one made me cry the most. so without further rant about my cry</span>
  <span id="freeText16710273669648898181" style="display:none">I CRIED. well i guess it's not a surprise, because i've known Ilana Tan as someone who can write a story that plays well with the reader's heart. and i think this book is BETTER than - if not as good as - the 4 Seasons series. the story is not that complicated actually, but the emotions are just unbelievable! i still can't believe how much i cried while finishing the book... i've been reading a lot of emotional books lately, but this one made me cry the most. so without further rant about my crying, here's the review. <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://thebookielooker.blogspot.com/2012/01/book-review-sunshine-becomes-you.html">http://thebookielooker.blogspot.com/2...</a></span>

<div id="review_283578997" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/283578997" />
    <a title="Tessa Intanya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2714486-tessa-intanya"><img alt="Tessa Intanya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442474325p2/2714486.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/283578997?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessa Intanya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessa Intanya" href="/user/show/2714486-tessa-intanya">Tessa Intanya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer283578997" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1721777725690406922">I finished reading this book last weekend. I enjoyed it. Not as much as I enjoyed Ms. Tan’s previous novels… I don’t think there’s any particular difference between ‘Sunshine Becomes You’ and her 4 books prior to this. It seems too formulaic. I can’t decide whether this is a good thing or a bad thing for a writer. Does that means that the writer has not develop their writing skill thru the course of time? Or does it simply means that the writer has found his/her style? But won’t that bore the re</span>
  <span id="freeText1721777725690406922" style="display:none">I finished reading this book last weekend. I enjoyed it. Not as much as I enjoyed Ms. Tan’s previous novels… I don’t think there’s any particular difference between ‘Sunshine Becomes You’ and her 4 books prior to this. It seems too formulaic. I can’t decide whether this is a good thing or a bad thing for a writer. Does that means that the writer has not develop their writing skill thru the course of time? Or does it simply means that the writer has found his/her style? But won’t that bore the readers? <br /><br />Regardless, I just appreciate Ilana Tan’s storytelling way that somehow captivates and gets to so many readers, including myself. It’s as if we’re watching a Japanese dorama, which I love to do in my spare time (That’s why for this particular book in my mind I got to cast Daniel Henney as the main male protagonist, Alex Hirano, then Kristen Kreuk as the vulnerable yet lovely, Mia Clark and Harry Shum Jr as Ray Hirano –fyi) <br /><br />The plotline of the story reminds me of 2 particular Hollywood movies: ‘Sweet November’ and ‘Love and Other Drugs’, since all female leads in those movies (and this book) discovers that they have terminal illness and tragically found love at the same time (talk about bad timing, rite?). But the story also vaguely reminds me of this 90s romantic drama entitled: ‘Return to Me’. All in all, like I’ve mentioned earlier, I enjoyed most part of the book. It was a light read that was quite fun to read during my spare times. Although the sad sentiment didn’t really move me to tears this time around (either I’ve turn bitter over the years or have I outgrown this kind of plotlines, I’m not sure), I liked it.<br /><br />I get confused a little though regarding Alex’s roots… His surname is Hirano (which is obviously Japanese), so I took it as being his father’s last name, rite? But in the book, it was mentioned that his grandparents from his dad side resides in New York too. Does that means they’re Americans (isn’t that a bit off?), or are they just simply Japanese New Yorkers? I dunno, maybe it’s my mistake. <br /><br />Anyways, if you have the time, just read it. It’s a quite nice romantic book to read during the last week of the month of love, as February is about to end soon.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1721777725690406922" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

So< when I found it last night in the bookstore I bought it immediately. I love Ilana's books. They are special for me because of her ability to teel, to write a story which make me want to read it more and more...   <span id="freeText3762448900428232095" style="display:none">Sunshine Becomes You. This book is about out of stock in my town and it's hard to find. So&lt; when I found it last night in the bookstore I bought it immediately. I love Ilana's books. They are special for me because of her ability to teel, to write a story which make me want to read it more and more... They are addicting.<br /><br /><br /><br />This book tells about a musician, Alex Hirano, and a dancer, Mia Clark. It is funny that they know and became close to each other because of a small accident. Yeah.. the readers can guess that they will fall in love in the end. And no, it's not like Autumn in Paris which has a hurtful fact that made the main characters can't be toghether and sad ending. And it is also not like Winter in Tokyo which has a very sweet moments and ending. Well, it was a combination maybe. There are the bitter-sweet moments and bitter-sweet ending. And I didn't have an idea that the ending could be like that. it surprised me.<br /><br /><br /><br />One more thing I like the most about Ilana is she can picture the men's personality. not by the exact description but by the conversations, their feelings and I think all of the men in her books acted nicely and they have a he-is-the-prince-charming personality. <br /><br /><br /><br />This book really can touch my emotion. I spent 6 hours straight to finish the book, I was curious with it. I love the story even though I a little bit disagree with the ending because I don't like the ending like that. I have a lesson I learnt about the book: Sometimes the bad things are the right things. A bit weird, is it?</span>

Mia accidentally</span>
  <span id="freeText3841104565105454959" style="display:none">Indonesian Review here:<br /><a href="http://thebookaddictdiaries.blogspot.com/2012/02/judul-sunshine-becomes-you-author-ilana.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bookaddict Diaries: Sunshine Becomes You</a><br /><s>I wished the story ends differently :(</s><br /><br />It stirs my heart, just like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4374400.If_I_Stay__If_I_Stay___1_" title="If I Stay (If I Stay, #1) by Gayle Forman" rel="nofollow noopener">If I Stay</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8492825.Where_She_Went__If_I_Stay___2_" title="Where She Went (If I Stay, #2) by Gayle Forman" rel="nofollow noopener">Where She Went</a> when I read it. It was beautiful, enchanting, and it made me love Ilana Tan even more. I read her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/58799-season-series" rel="nofollow noopener">Season Series</a> and I was beyond fascinated, loving the way Ilana Tan creates a story in other countries, but still mentioning Indonesia in the process.<br /><br />Alex Hirano is a pianist, and he meets Mia Clark, a contemporary dancer. Mia accidentally falls from the stairs and breaks Alex's wrist. Guilty, Mia insists to help Alex in his apartment.<br /><br />Soon, Alex starts to realize that he's head over heels with this girl. But what if he finds out Mia's most hidden secret, one she's not willing to share?<br /><br />I gave it a chance (it's rare for me to pick up an Indonesian book) because of the <b>'New York'</b> words on the cover. I admit I adore the city, and I was curious to see how an Indonesia writer describes New York. I was a bit disappointed, though, because the description isn't detailed.</span>

<div id="review_463440001" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/463440001" />
    <a title="Bernadeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14906631-bernadeth"><img alt="Bernadeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353882978p2/14906631.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/463440001?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bernadeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bernadeth" href="/user/show/14906631-bernadeth">Bernadeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14906631-bernadeth?shelf=teenlit">teenlit</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer463440001" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6614883735575825786">I've always like the way Ilana Tan express her story. She doesn't use complicated words, nor street words, and that makes her books look smart. <br/><br/>Alex Hirano (as expected from the name) adalah pianis terkenal keturunan Jepang-Amerika. He's that cold-secretly-kind-hearted guy. Sedangkan Mia Clark (yg juga keturunan Asia-Amerika) adalah perempuan menarik berhati lembut dan bekerja sebagai penari kontemporer. Their love story went smoothly from irritation to actually fall in love to each other. Reali</span>
  <span id="freeText6614883735575825786" style="display:none">I've always like the way Ilana Tan express her story. She doesn't use complicated words, nor street words, and that makes her books look smart. <br /><br />Alex Hirano (as expected from the name) adalah pianis terkenal keturunan Jepang-Amerika. He's that cold-secretly-kind-hearted guy. Sedangkan Mia Clark (yg juga keturunan Asia-Amerika) adalah perempuan menarik berhati lembut dan bekerja sebagai penari kontemporer. Their love story went smoothly from irritation to actually fall in love to each other. Realistis, memang, tetapi sedikit terlalu teenlit-like (terutama bagian tabrakan di chapter awal). Buku ini termasuk easy to read, ceritanya simple tapi ga pasaran. Sebenernya alasan kenapa mungkin orang2 ga terlalu absorb ke buku ini adalah karena twist di ending caused a huge emotional breakdown for everyone (and I'm one of them). When Alex told Ray his feelings to Mia, I almost cried. Sedihnya jadi double karena Mia sendiri ga rela kalah sama penyakitnya #tragis<br /><br />Sebenernya dibandingin Autumn in Paris, Sunshine Becomes You ga nelangsa2 amat. Cuma karena saya expect happy ending, jadinya malah yaoming face. TAPI! Ini memang layak dikoleksi. It's nearly impossible to hate the characters in it. Lagipula, mudah untuk membayangkan sosok Alex dan Mia. Ini bagus kyny klo diadaptasi jadi film. A must read for romance novel worshippers; sama sekali ga direkomendasikan buat yg menderita penyakit ga-bisa-move-on-kalo-endingnya-bukan-happily-ever-after. <br /><br />Great job buat Ilana Tan. More books please! :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="6614883735575825786" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_516819737" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/516819737" />
    <a title="Odilia Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16546206-odilia-christy"><img alt="Odilia Christy" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/516819737?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Odilia Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Odilia Christy" href="/user/show/16546206-odilia-christy">Odilia Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer516819737" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9399616500548447247">No doubt, this is one of the best novels I have ever read. Totally love it. Because of this book, I went back to the book store the day after I bought this book to buy other novels by Ilana Tan.<br/>I really like the way Ilana tell the story; ot was super easy and light. Too bad I left this book back in my home, which is 20 hours away by plane. I really want to re-read this amazing masterpiece.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Y4OFKYyuLxHFoq+qAdV6VFZdYNUSdfySv5kLfTlm8SqOG46nhqviNp4+QYqQlfDA1kyix3siWS10cyc3P9gmaA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GtS8i7alnrvad15Rq0qYzaj6bVeaG5ZMJ/XtvRoqwYf3TLcFvKBTnIHrsHE6ChJZKOuvRfNMM/PsH8H3HJQWxQ==')})
  }
//]]>

Mereka adalah Arial yang paling tampan, Riani sebagai satu-satunya wanita dalam kelompok itu, Zafran yang berlagak sepe<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText3897498858213902568\" style=\"display:none\">Bestseller book di Gramedia Bookstore selama 2 tahun berturut-turut!\n\nLima sahabat telah menjalin persahabatan selama tujuh tahun. Mereka adalah Arial yang paling tampan, Riani sebagai satu-satunya wanita dalam kelompok itu, Zafran yang berlagak seperti seorang penyair, Ian yang paling subur badannya, dan Genta yang dianggap sebagai leader dalam kelompok itu. Kegemaran mereka adalah mengeksekusi hal-hal yang tidak mungkin dan mencoba segala hal, mulai dari kafe paling terkenal di Jakarta, sampai nonton layar tancap. Semuanya penggemar film, dari film Hollywood sampai film yang nggak kelas—kecuali film India karena mereka punya prinsip bahwa semua persoalan di dunia atau masalah pasti ada jalan keluarnya, tapi bukan dalam bentuk joget.\n\nSuatu saat, karena terdorong oleh rasa bosan di antara satu dan yang lain, mereka memutuskan untuk tidak saling berkomunikasi dan bertemu satu sama lain selama tiga bulan. Selama tiga bulan berpisah itulah telah terjadi banyak hal yang membuat hati mereka lebih kaya dari sebelumnya. Pertemuan setelah tiga bulan yang penuh dengan rasa kangen akhirnya terjadi dan dirayakan dengan sebuah perjalanan. Sebuah perjalanan yang penuh dengan keyakinan, mimpi, cita-cita, dan cinta. Sebuah perjalanan yang telah mengubah mereka menjadi manusia sesungguhnya, bukan Cuma seonggok daging yang bisa berbicara, berjalan, dan punya nama.\n\n“Ada yang pernah bilang kalau idealisme adalah kemewahan terakhir yang dimiliki oleh generasi muda….”  <\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"3897498858213902568\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n    <\/div>\n\n           <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>

<a href="/author/show/696355.Ilana_Tan">Ilana Tan
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>

followers

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer743989620713425646">Ilana Tan adalah seorang novelis Indonesia yang dikenal karena menulis 4 novel roman yang masing-masing novelnya disajikan dengan cerita yang latarnya berbeda-beda. Novel Ilana Tan memiliki keunikan, yaitu tokoh-tokoh dari novel yang satu dengan novel yang lainnya saling berkaitan.[1]<br/>Novel pertamanya berjudul Summer in Seoul, novel keduanya berjudul Autumn in Paris, novel ketiganya berjudul Winter</span>
  <span id="freeText743989620713425646" style="display:none">Ilana Tan adalah seorang novelis Indonesia yang dikenal karena menulis 4 novel roman yang masing-masing novelnya disajikan dengan cerita yang latarnya berbeda-beda. Novel Ilana Tan memiliki keunikan, yaitu tokoh-tokoh dari novel yang satu dengan novel yang lainnya saling berkaitan.[1]<br />Novel pertamanya berjudul Summer in Seoul, novel keduanya berjudul Autumn in Paris, novel ketiganya berjudul Winter in Tokyo dan novel keempatnya berjudul Spring in London. Masing-masing novel diceritakan di kota-kota besar di dunia, yaitu Seoul (Korea Selatan), Paris (Perancis), Tokyo (Jepang), dan London (Inggris). Dan masing-masing novel diceritakan di musim yang berbeda; Summer (musim panas), Autumn (musim gugur), Winter (musim dingin), dan Spring (musim semi).</span>
  <a data-text-id="743989620713425646" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
